## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: chemical kinetics
**Analysis**: This task models the rate of change of a chemical species concentration dA/dt as a function of time and concentration, which is the fundamental problem of chemical reaction kinetics involving rate laws of varying order and complexity.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Zero-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 (constant rate, independent of concentration)
- First-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A (radioactive decay, unimolecular decomposition)
- Second-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 (bimolecular reaction of same species)
- nth-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 (general power-law rate law)
- Mixed-order with offset: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 + c2 (rate law with constant production term)
- Reversible first-order: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 (first-order forward with zero-order reverse or equilibrium shift)
- Michaelis-Menten type: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A) (enzyme kinetics, saturation kinetics)
- Substrate inhibition: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A + c2 * A**2) (enzyme kinetics with inhibition)
- Autocatalytic: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (logistic-type autocatalytic reaction)
- Time-dependent rate: dA_dt = c0 * A * exp(c1 * t) (time-varying rate constant, e.g., temperature ramp)
- Parallel reactions: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2 (simultaneous first and second order pathways)
- Fractional order with time: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 + c2 * t (complex mechanism with time-dependent source)
- Langmuir-Hinshelwood: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A)**2 (surface-catalyzed reaction kinetics)
- Cooperative kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 / (c2 + A**c1) (Hill-type cooperative binding/reaction)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Integer or half-integer power of concentration → elementary or pseudo-elementary reaction step with defined molecularity
- Rational function of concentration (numerator/denominator polynomial in A) → enzyme or surface catalysis mechanism with adsorption-desorption equilibria
- Linear dependence on A with nonzero intercept → reversible reaction with back-reaction or constant production/inflow
- Product of A and (constant - A) → autocatalytic or logistic reaction where product catalyzes its own formation
- Explicit time dependence multiplied by concentration term → time-varying external conditions (temperature ramp, light intensity variation, fed-batch reactor)
- Sum of multiple power-law terms in A → parallel competing reaction pathways with different orders
- Concentration in denominator squared → surface reaction with competitive adsorption or substrate inhibition
- Exponential function of time multiplying a rate law → Arrhenius-type temperature programming or photochemical intensity variation over time
